				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Lobet Gott in seinen Reichen, BWV 11 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="wp_header">
<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>2 parts (in 11 movements)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1735 in Leipzig
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>

</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Lobet Gott in seinen Reichen

</th>

</td></tr>
<tr>

</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Bach,_Johann_Sebastian" title="Category:Bach, Johann Sebastian">Bach, Johann Sebastian</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Opus/Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">Op./Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>BWV 11&#160;; BC D 9
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>IJB 376
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Key
</th>
<td>D major
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>2 parts (in 11 movements):
<ul><li><b>Prima Parte</b>
</li></ul>
<dl><dd>1. Chorus: Lobet Gott in seinen Reichen (D&#160;major)
</dd><dd>2. Recitative (tenor): Der Herr Jesus hub seine Hände auf
</dd><dd>3. Recitative (bass): Ach, Jesu, ist dein Abschied schon so nah?
</dd><dd>4. Aria (alto): Ach, bleibe doch, mein liebstes Leben (A&#160;minor)
</dd><dd>5. Recitative (tenor): Und ward aufgehoben zusehends
</dd><dd>6. Chorale: Nun lieget alles unter dir (D&#160;major)
</dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>Secondo Parte</b> 
</li></ul>
<dl><dd>7. Recitative (tenor and bass): Und da sie ihm nachsahen gen Himmel fahren
</dd><dd>8. Recitative (soprano): Ach ja! so komme bald zurück
</dd><dd>9. Recitative (tenor): Sie aber beteten ihn an
</dd><dd>10. Aria (soprano): Jesu, deine Gnadenblicke (G&#160;major)
</dd><dd>11. Chorale: Wenn soll es doch geschehen (D&#160;major)
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Year/Date of Composition</span><span class="ms555">Y/D of Comp.</span>
</th>
<td>1735 in Leipzig
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Perf<span class="mh555">ormance</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1735-05-19 in Leipzig
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Pub<span class="mh555">lication</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1852 (BGA)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Librettist
</th>
<td><i>see below</i>
<dl><dd><a href="/wiki/Category:Henrici,_Christian_Friedrich" title="Category:Henrici, Christian Friedrich">Christian Friedrich Henrici</a> (1700-1764) <i>[as Picander]</i> <br /><a href="/wiki/Category:Anonymous" title="Category:Anonymous">Anonymous</a> (Nos.1, 3-4, 8, 10)<br />Luke 24: 50-51 (No.2)<br />Acts 1: 9 (No.5)<br />Mark 16: 19 (No.5)<br />Acts 1: 10-11 (No.7)<br />Luke 24: 52 (No.8)<br />Acts 1: 12 (No.8)
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>
<tr>

</th>
<td>German
</td></tr>
